came under British, French, and Spanish control.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bb07c24"><p class="cl-9bb03534"><span class="cl-9bb028f0">No</span><span class="cl-9bb028f0"> </span><span in 1774.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bb07c06"><p class="cl-9bb03534"><span class="cl-9bb028f0">No</span><span class="cl-9bb028f0"> </span><span class="cl-9bb028f0">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr support for U.K. rights in the Falklands.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bb07c06"><p class="cl-9bb03534"><span class="cl-9bb02904">United</span><span class="cl-9bb02904"> </span><span 1983.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd8247c"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">No</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-9bd7ee6c">Background and Pre-crisisSudan and Libya experienced a basic change in political regime almost simultaneously: a seizure of power by Brigadier-General Numeiri in Khartoum in May 1969; and a coup d'tat led by Colonel Qaddhafi in Tripoli in September 1969, overthrowing the monarchy.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd824ae"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span ouster in 1985; and Qaddhafi, who is still in power.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd8247c"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">No</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bd824af"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">340.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd824ae"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">However, the two regimes differed markedly: Numeiri was pro-West; and Qaddhafi projected a messianic role, designed to transform the Arab world.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd824ae"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">No</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span 1980s.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd8247c"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">No</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-9bd7ee6c">Sudan perceived continuous attempts at subversion by Qaddhafi, aimed at expanding his influence in Africa and the Arab world through mergers, as with Chad, Egypt, and Tunisia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd824ae"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">No</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr the Soviet Union were concentrated near the border.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd824ae"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bd7ee80">Libya</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee80"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee80">area;fortify</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c">toward</span><span class="cl-9bd7ee6c"> </span><span February, of a Libyan plan to overthrow the Numeiri regime triggered a crisis for Sudan and Egypt.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bd8247c"><p class="cl-9bd7f948"><span class="cl-9bf5d4af"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">Long before the coup there had been speculation in Grenada that the U.S. was planning some form of military intervention, especially after President Reagan, on 23 March 1983, described the island's regime as a "threat to the security of the United States."</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4af"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">No</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c"> </span><span class="cl-9bf5919c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bf5d4ae"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">343.19</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4a4"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">Washington had expressed anxiety over Cuban participation in the construction of the Point Salinas international airport, viewing it as a potential military base for Soviet-bloc forces in the Americas.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4a4"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf591a6">United</span><span class="cl-9bf591a6"> </span><span class="cl-9bf591a6">States</span><span class="cl-9bf591a6"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-9bf591a6">this</span><span class="cl-9bf591a6"> </span><span class="cl-9bf591a6">sentence</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c">.</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c"> </span><span class="cl-9bf5919c">343.20</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4af"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">Relations between the U.S. and Grenada had been further strained by the growing tension between the Reagan administration and the Sandinista regime in Nicaragua, especially after joint U.S.-Honduras military maneuvers in August.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4af"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf5919c">No</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c"> </span><span class="cl-9bf5919c">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td by supporters but was quickly recaptured; in the firing that ensued, an estimated 200 persons were killed or wounded by Austin's troops.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bf5d4a4"><p class="cl-9bf59c96"><span class="cl-9bf591a6">Grenada</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c"> </span><span class="cl-9bf5919c">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bf5919c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.3</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">The most crucial were war games involving the planned use of nuclear weapons in both "first-strike" and retaliation scenarios.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">No</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb864"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.4</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">Like the Warsaw Pact, NATO had conducted war games before, but its 1983 nuclear exercise, Able Archer, was more extensive than ever before.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">No</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.5</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">The Soviet misperception of the U.S.'s and NATO's intentions was influenced by its image of the Reagan administration as unpredictable, with a president who was willing to use force to protect and enhance U.S. "national interests."</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">No</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb864"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">In the 18 months before Exercise Able Archer the U.S. had dispatched forces to Lebanon.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">United</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">States</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">of</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">America</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">deployment</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">to</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">area;exercise;mobilization</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">toward</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Lebanon</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">Soviet mistrust and concern were also reinforced by an incident on 1 September 1983, when a Soviet fighter plane shot down a Korean airliner, KAL-007, which penetrated deep into Soviet airspace while on a flight from Alaska to Seoul; all passengers and crew were killed, including 60 Americans.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">in</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">this</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">sentence</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">attack</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">toward</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">United</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">States</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">of</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">America;South</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Korea</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb864"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">This incident caused deep concern in the U.S. Reagan later wrote in his memoirs: "If anything, the KAL incident demonstrated how close the world had come to the precipice and how much we needed nuclear arms control.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">United</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">States</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">of</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">America</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">experienced</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">a</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">7</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.9</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">" Given this series of events, all of which were perceived in the Soviet prism as hostile and threatening, the sudden discovery of Exercise Able Archer was interpreted as ominous by Soviet decision makers.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">experienced</span><span class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">On 2 November 1983 NATO began a military exercise code-named Able Archer.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">NATO</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">NATO</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">exercise</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.11</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">The large-scale war game embraced all NATO territory from Norway to Turkey between 2 and 11 November and included large amounts of arms and combat equipment.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">No</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb864"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.12</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">Its aim was to test nuclear release mechanisms in case of a nuclear first strike against the Soviet bloc.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">No</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.13</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">Able Archer was misperceived by the USSR as preparation for, not a simulation of, a nuclear attack by the West.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">sentence</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">NATO</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span crisis for the USSR -- the closest the two superpowers came to a direct nuclear confrontation since the Cuban Missile crisis in 1962.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb863"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Union</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9bfeb862"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">344.15</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">During the exercise, U.S. intelligence, monitoring Soviet communications, was alarmed to hear that the USSR was expecting -- and preparing for -- a nuclear war in a short time.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">United</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe8072">The USSR first responded on 5 November, sending messages to the KGB residencies in Europe to warn of a Western surprise attack and ordering them to increase their vigilance.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9bfeb858"><p class="cl-9bfe8ba8"><span class="cl-9bfe807c">Soviet</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span </span><span class="cl-9bfe8072">initiated</span><span class="cl-9bfe8072"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">raise</span><span class="cl-9bfe807c"> </span><span class="cl-9bfe807c">in</span><span north.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c15a05e"><p class="cl-9c1576ba"><span class="cl-9c156b98">No</span><span class="cl-9c156b98"> </span><span class="cl-9c156b98">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-9c268a4a">Union</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">initiated</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a4a">military</span><span class="cl-9c268a4a"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a4a">cooperation</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">toward</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a4a">Kuwait</span><span class="cl-9c268a40">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce39"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.33</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">This marked the end of the Basra-Kharg Island crisis as a whole; but the war continued unabated for another four years.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce43"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.34</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">As in earlier phases of the Iran/Iraq War, all attempts to end the war -- by the UN, the Gulf states, the Non-Aligned Movement, and various Islamic organizations -- failed, though, as noted, the UN Secretary-General arranged a brief moratorium on the bombing of civilian areas.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce39"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.35</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">France continued to be a major arms supplier to Iraq, whose war effort was heavily financed by Kuwait and Sa'udi Arabia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce43"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.36</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">The U.S. goal throughout Gulf War I was to keep the Strait of Hormuz open to the steady flow of oil to its allies in Europe and Japan.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce39"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.37</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">Secretly it provided Iraq with valuable technological assistance and intelligence information throughout the war, and antiaircraft missiles and a naval escort for Sa'udi ships.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce43"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.38</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">The USSR provided arms to Iraq, notably SS-12 ground-to-ground missiles.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce39"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.39</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">Other suppliers of military equipment to Iraq were Egypt, Brazil, China, and Chile.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce43"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.40</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">Except for Syria, the Arab world supported Iraq: both the Gulf Cooperation Council and the Arab League condemned Iran.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c26ce39"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">348.41</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">And the latter sought UN intervention.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce38"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span Gulf.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c26ce42"><p class="cl-9c2695d0"><span class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr class="cl-9c268a40">No</span><span class="cl-9c268a40"> </span><span class="cl-9c268a40">events.</span></p></td></tr></tbody></table></div>

class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">military</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">cooperation;unspecified</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">cooperation</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">toward</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">Cambodia</span><span class="cl-9c427f20">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c42ae97"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">351.5</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">Thus the crisis generated by Vietnam's incursion into Thailand in March 1984 was an extension of the protracted conflict between Vietnam and Cambodia.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">No</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">events.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c42aeb4"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">351.6</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae98"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">A crisis was triggered for Thailand on 25 March 1984 by the intrusion of Vietnamese troops into its territory in pursuit of Khmer Rouge Cambodian rebels: Vietnam's cross-border raid, along with Thai military and civilian casualties, was perceived as seriously undermining Thailand's security.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae98"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f2a">Thailand</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">experienced</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">a</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">start</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">of</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">crisis</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">about</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">act</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">in</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">this</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">sentence</span><span class="cl-9c427f20">.</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">Vietnam</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">initiated</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">border</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">violation</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">toward</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">Thailand</span><span class="cl-9c427f20">.</span></p></td></tr><tr style="overflow-wrap:break-word;"><td class="cl-9c42ae97"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">351.7</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">Bangkok responded quickly along two paths: a military effort to force the Vietnamese back into Kampuchea; and a diplomatic offensive in both Washington and the UN.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f2a">Thailand</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f20">initiated</span><span class="cl-9c427f20">351.8</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae98"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">The first included minor clashes in the area of the Khmer Rouge camp, the Chong Phra Palai Pass linking Kampuchea and Thailand.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae98"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">No</span><span class="cl-9c427f20"> </span><span class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f20">The second led to tangible U.S. support.</span></p></td><td class="cl-9c42ae96"><p class="cl-9c428a10"><span class="cl-9c427f2a">United</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">States</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">of</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">general</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">political</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">support</span><span </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">sentence</span><span class="cl-9c427f2a"> </span><span class="cl-9c427f2a">11</span><span class="cl-9c427f20">.</span></p></td></tr><tr
